	desc = USA.4.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.4.a

	}
}

	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			70 = { USA = { country_event = { id = USA.25 } } }
			30 = { USA = { country_event = { id = USA.26 } } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.24.a
	}
}

#Mccormack decides whether or not he wants to try and pull the RDs together
country_event = {
	#id = USA.33
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.33"}
	title = USA.33.t
	desc = USA.33.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rd_generic1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #we must try
		name = USA.33.a
		add_political_power = -25
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_to_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = mccormack_against_npp }
		USA_reload_nixon_tree = yes
	}
	option = { #it's not my place
		name = USA.33.b
		add_political_power = 50
	}
}

country_event = { #Fischer becomes Fasher
	id = USA.34
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.34"}
	title = USA.34.t
	desc = USA.34.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_rd_generic1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #keep tabs
		name = USA.34.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = USA.35
				days = 90
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #who cares lol
		name = USA.34.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #fuk u
		name = USA.34.c
		country_event = {
			id = USA.35
			days = 3
		}
	}
}

 #Join the South African war?
country_event = {
	id = USA.40
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.40"}
	title = USA.40.t
	desc = USA.40.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_south_african_war_saf_soldier

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.40.a
		set_global_flag = south_african_war #THIS IS THE ORIGIN IS THIS FLAG!!!!
		set_country_flag = USA_In_The_SAF_WAR
		set_country_flag = USA_Has_Been_In_the_SAF_WAR
		set_country_flag = will_send_troops
		TNO_fopo_add_saw_tab = yes
		set_global_flag = south_african_war_happening
		set_technology = {
			gunship_1966 = 1
		}
		SAF = {
			set_country_flag = USA_entered_war
			country_event = {
				id = SAFWAR.7
				days = 4
			}
			country_event = {
				id = SAF.41
				days = 2
			}
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = USA_african_adventure
			days = 150
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA.41 days = 4 } #
			country_event = { id = USA.culture.29 days = 137 } #Anti war culture
			country_event = { id = USA.culture.33 days = 183 } #Hard Hat riots
			country_event = { id = SAFWAR.29 days = 364 }
			SAF = {
				#add_named_threat = {
				#	threat = 25
				#	name = threat.10.t
				#}
			}
			SAF = {
				SAW_rubberband_effect = yes
				SAW_update_rubberband = yes
				log = "[?GetName] SAF.SAW_surrender = [?THIS.SAW_surrender] - LAZER"
			}
			USA = {
				SAW_rubberband_effect = yes
				SAW_update_rubberband = yes
				log = "[?GetName] SAF.SAW_surrender = [?THIS.SAW_surrender] - LAZER"
			}
			GRO = {
				SAW_rubberband_effect = yes
				SAW_update_rubberband = yes
				log = "[?GetName] GRO.SAW_surrender = [?THIS.SAW_surrender] - LAZER"
			}
			ANG = {
				SAW_rubberband_effect = yes
				SAW_update_rubberband = yes
				log = "[?GetName] ANG.SAW_surrender = [?THIS.SAW_surrender] - LAZER"
			}
			COG = {
				SAW_rubberband_effect = yes
				SAW_update_rubberband = yes
				log = "[?GetName] COG.SAW_surrender = [?THIS.SAW_surrender] - LAZER"
			}
			country_event = { id = USA.209 days = 28 }
			if = { #Experimental ai code
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { target = SAF }
				TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_2 = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = "TNO_increase_volunteers_SAF_2"
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { target = SAF }
				TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_2 = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = "TNO_increase_volunteers_SAF_2"
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = USA.ct.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.ct.1" }

	desc = USA.ct.1.desc
 	picture = GFX_report_event_germania_2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Sweet sweet sweet, lets get down to buisness
		name = USA.ct.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

	}
}

country_event = { #South African ambassador meets with the Americans, assured that this time they actually have shit to say. For once they don't press on joining the OFN, and get down to buisness in terms of ensuring SAF's protection
	id = USA.ct.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.ct.2" }
	title = USA.ct.2.t
	desc = USA.ct.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_east_africa_quelimane

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Awesome!
		name = USA.ct.2.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SAF
			modifier = USA_South_africa_Working_Together
		}
		SAF = {
			add_stability = 0.02
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = USA modifier = USA_South_africa_Working_Together}
		}
	}
}

}

 #UNLOCK SAF OFN TREE
country_event = {
	id = USA.41
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.41"}
	title = USA.41.t
	desc = USA.41.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.41.a
		set_country_flag = USA_sa_ofn
		add_to_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
		USA_reload_nixon_tree = yes
	}
}

country_event = {#Form the CAR?
	id = USA.51
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.51"}
	title = USA.51.t
	desc = USA.51.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Form the CAR
		name = USA.51.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 30 
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                has_game_rule = { rule = CAR_FATE_PATH option = CAR_FATE_PATH_NO }
            }
			modifier = {
				SAF = {
					NOT = {
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		TNO_fopo_add_saf_reconstruction_conflict_tab = yes
		set_global_flag = CAR_FORMED
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = OFN_AFR_MANDATE.1 days = 1 }
			OFN_CAR_Initialize = yes
		}
	}
	option = { #Keep the three administrations
		name = USA.51.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 60 
		    modifier = {
                factor = 0
                has_game_rule = { rule = CAR_FATE_PATH option = CAR_FATE_PATH_YES }
            }
		}	
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA.effects.18 days = 3 }
			country_event = { id = OFN_AFR_MANDATE.0 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

		name = USA.55.a
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_idea = USA_conscription_riot } }
			add_ideas = USA_conscription_riot
		}
 		#hidden_effect = {
 		#	country_event = { id = USA.53 days = 8 }
 		#}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_npp_5_increase
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = US_election_state }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#US invites SAF to the OFN
country_event = {
	id = USA.61
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.61"}
	title = USA.61.t
	desc = USA.61.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_pentagon
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.61.a
		USA = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				add_to_faction = SAF
				add_to_array = { OFN_members = SAF }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.61.b
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

	}

		name = USA.67.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = USA }
			is_in_faction_with = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.67.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = USA
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Civil Rights Act - veto
news_event = {
	id = USA.68
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.68"}
	title = USA.68.t
	desc = USA.68.desc
	picture = GFX_news_event_veto_cra
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.68.a
		trigger = { tag = USA }
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 5 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_defectors_2
		custom_effect_tooltip = NPP_shift_left
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_nixon_cra_veto
		add_ideas = USA_North_Discontent_1
		set_variable = { USA_North_Discontent_ticker = 0 }
		set_variable = { USA_North_Discontent_change = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			US_elections_calculate_country_vars = yes
			country_event = {
				id = USA.1804
				days = 2555
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.325 }
				if = { #Give a bigger bonus to Yankee states
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 82 } }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.55 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
				else = {
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.45 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = { #Polarized against NPP Center/Left
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African-American
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.1 }
				if = { #Give a bigger bonus to Dixie states
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 83 } }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = -0.3 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
				else = {
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = -0.1 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = { #The Republicans are weaker everywhere, which the Democrats make up for
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }

				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.1 }
				if = { #Give a bigger bonus to Yankee states
					limit = { check_variable = { nationality = 83 } }
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.225 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
				else = {
					multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.1 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			}
			396 = { # Indiana
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.32 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.32 }
				set_variable = { senator_1 = 4 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_R_name = 1 }
			}

			388 = { # Montana
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.35 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.37 }
				set_variable = { senator_2 = 4 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_D_name = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 }
			}

			359 = { # New Jersey
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.32 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.32 }
				set_variable = { senator_1 = 4 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_R_name = 1 }
			}
			358 = { # New York
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.28 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.28 }
				set_variable = { senator_1 = 4 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_R_name = 1 }
			}
			360 = { # Pennsylvania
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.33 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.27 } # Removed change of senator, this should flip in 64
			}
			948 = { # Rhode Island
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.33 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.25 }
				set_variable = { senator_2 = 4 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_R_name = 1 }
				add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 }
			}

			}

				set_variable = { senator_2 = 4 }

			}

#Nixon resigns
country_event = {
	id = USA.103
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.103"}
	title = USA.103.t
	desc = USA.103.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_nixon_v_for_victory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.103.a

		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = { id = USA.420 }
			}
			country_event = { id = USA.104 days = 62 }
			country_event = { id = USA.early_flavor.3 days = 6 }
			country_event = { id = USA.167 days = 20 }
		}

		effect_tooltip = {
			retire_country_leader = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }

		subtract_from_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 5 }
		clr_country_flag = USA_60_R_RD
		set_country_flag = USA_nixon_impeached
		set_country_flag = USA_JFK_is_president
		USA_reload_nixon_tree = yes
		hidden_effect = {

			US_elections_calculate_country_vars = yes
			remove_ideas = USA_John_F_Kennedy_dep
			add_ideas = USA_John_McCormack_dep
			promote_character = USA_John_McCormack

			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = conservative_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_societal_unity
			add_to_variable = { USA_unity = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				463 = { # Alaska (NPPC)
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.15 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.15 }
					set_variable = { senator_1 = 4 }
					add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_R_name = 1 } # We don't change the C-NPP name because it's already set
				}

				377 = { # Arizona (NPPFR)
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.15 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.15 }
					set_variable = { senator_1 = 6 }
					add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_D_name = 1 } # We don't change the FR-NPP name because it's already set
				}

				376 = { # New Mexico (NPPC)
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.15 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.15 }
					set_variable = { senator_2 = 4 }
					add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_R_name = 1 } # We don't change the C-NPP name because it's already set
				}

				381 = { # Wyoming (NPPFR)
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.25 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.25 }
					set_variable = { senator_2 = 6 }
					add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_D_name = 1 } # We don't change the FR-NPP name because it's already set
				}
				US_elections_calculate_country_vars = yes
				set_variable = { presidents_party = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#Kennedy assassinated
country_event = {
	id = USA.104
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.104"}
	title = USA.104.t
	desc = USA.104.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress_2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.104.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			set_politics = { ruling_party = liberal_democracy }
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = liberal_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		set_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 0	}
		USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
		add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1}

		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = USA_the_american_depression_4
			add_idea = USA_the_american_depression_5
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_societal_unity_large
		add_to_variable = { USA_unity = -2 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_passed }
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_CRA_progress_stalls
			hidden_effect = {
				TNO_worsen_vote_franchise_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
				TNO_worsen_minorities_policy_effectiveness_monthly_med = yes
				country_event = { id = USA.1040 days = 13 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = { id = USA.421 }
			}
			remove_ideas = USA_John_McCormack_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Carl_Hayden_dep
			promote_character = USA_Wallace_F_Bennett

			#country_event = { id = USA.33 days = 7 }
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_passed
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.133 days = 21 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_civil_rights_blocked
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.133 days = 21 }
				country_event = { id = USA.early_flavor.4 days = 15 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = USA_nixon_neutral
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.134 days = 21 }
				country_event = { id = USA.early_flavor.4 days = 15 }
			}
			US_elections_calculate_country_vars = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_JFK_killed
			clr_country_flag = USA_JFK_is_president
			set_country_flag = mccormack_against_npp
			clr_country_flag = USA_initial_tree_flag
			set_country_flag = mccormack_is_president
			USA_reload_nixon_tree = yes
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = USA.135
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.135"}
	title = USA.135.t
	desc = USA.135.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_capitol_building2

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = currently_campaigning
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.12 days = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.136 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Bennett"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.137 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Johnson"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.138 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Wallace"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.139 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1964 elections: Kennedy"
			}
			set_variable = { US_debt_expectation = debt_to_GDP_ratio}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Wallace F. Bennett
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 } }
		name = USA.135.a
	}
	option = { #LBJ
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 } }
		name = USA.135.b
	}
	option = { #George Wallace
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 } }
		name = USA.135.c
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = wallace.629 days = 13 } }
	}
	option = { #RFK
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 } }
		name = USA.135.d
	}
}

country_event = {

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.137"}
	title = USA.137.t
	desc = USA.137.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_LBJ_Inaug

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter  min = 0 }
			#set_country_flag = has_government = social_democracy
			set_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD
			set_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD_Past
			375 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_R_name = 1 } } # LBJ can't be the senator and President - I can't? Watch me
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = liberal_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			promote_character = USA_Lyndon_B_Johnson
			promote_character = USA_Henry_M_Jackson
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.702
					days = 1
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Edmund_Muskie_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Dean_Rusk_pol
			add_ideas = USA_Henry_Fowler_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Robert_McNamara_mil
			952 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_D_name = 1 } } # Muskie no longer uses the seat
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_64_tree_available
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_In_The_SAF_WAR }
				country_event = {
					id = RD_SAF.11
					days = 1
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = USA_LBJ_64
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.137.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_johnson_elected_64_tooltip
	}
}

#Wallace Inauguration Day 1965 what have you done
country_event = {
	id = USA.138
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.138"}
	title = USA.138.t
	desc = USA.138.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_wallace_and_lemay

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_64_tree_available
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_In_The_SAF_WAR }
				set_country_flag = USA_show_south_africa_tree
			}
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = USA_WAL_64
				keep_completed = yes
			}
			country_event = { ## Reload bennett CRA calculator
				id = wallace.630
				days = 660
			}
			# country_event = { id = wallace.1 days = 1 }
			retire_country_leader = yes
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter  min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
			set_country_flag = USA_NPP_64_SAF_war
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			promote_character = USA_Lyndon_B_Johnson
			promote_character = USA_Henry_M_Jackson
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.704
					days = 1
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Curtis_LeMay_dep
			add_ideas = USA_J_William_Fulbright_pol
			add_ideas = USA_Wilbur_Mills_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Robert_Byrd_mil
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = wallace.633 days = 17 } }
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.138.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_wallace_elected_64_tooltip
	}
}

#RFK Inauguration Day 1965
country_event = {
	id = USA.139
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.139"}
	title = USA.139.t
	desc = USA.139.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_RFK_Inaug

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes

			set_global_flag = USA_NPP_64_SAF_war
			set_country_flag = USA_NPP_64_SAF_war

			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter  min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP_Past
			set_country_flag = USA_NPP_64_SAF_war
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = social_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			promote_character = USA_Lyndon_B_Johnson
			promote_character = USA_Robert_F_Kennedy
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.703
					days = 1
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_64_tree_available
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_In_The_SAF_WAR }
				set_country_flag = USA_show_south_africa_tree
			}
			load_focus_tree = USA_RFK_64
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Hubert_Humphrey_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Generic_Vacant_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Generic_Vacant_for
			add_ideas = USA_Generic_Vacant_sec
			391 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 } } # Humphrey abandons his seat
			USA_RFK_flavor1 = yes
			set_variable = { RFK_brink = 4 }

			# Flavor
			if = {
				limit = { is_RD_in_control = yes }
				country_event = { id = strom.flavor.2 days = 3 } 
			} else = {
				country_event = { id = strom.flavor.1 days = 3 } 
			}
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 4 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.139.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_RFK_elected_64_tooltip
	}
}

#Reserving USA.142 for the Hope Massacre event

country_event = { #Alaska earthquake
	id = USA.143
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.143"}
	title = USA.143.t
	desc = USA.143.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_color

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.143.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_64_alaska_earthquake
		add_political_power = -10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = liberal_democracy
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		463 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 2
			}
			add_manpower = -139
		}
		463 = {
			random_list = {
				40 = {
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05}
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_RD_popularity_low
				}
				60 = {
					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.1 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
					custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows_low
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 160 - Maggie Smith
country_event = { #Chase-Smith Inauguration
	id = USA.160
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.160"}
	title = USA.160.t
	desc = USA.160.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_presidential_podium

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
			promote_character = USA_Margaret_Chase_Smith
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.714
					days = 1
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter  min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP_Past
			952 = { set_variable = { senator_2_NPP_FR_name = 1 } }
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Spiro_Agnew_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Jeane_Kirkpatrick_pol
			add_ideas = USA_Caspar_Weinberger_eco
			add_ideas = USA_John_Stennis_mil
			361 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_FR_name = 1 } } # Spiro Agnew Abandons seat
			370 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_FR_name = 1 } } # John Stennis Abandons seat
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_68_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_MCS_68
			if = { #Check if the response mission should activate
				limit = { #Either LBJ or RFK was POTUS
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP_Past
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			}
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = USA.neo_silver.1 days = 117 } }
			mcs_faction_setup = yes
			mcs_influence_calculation = yes
			mcs_update_party_display_debug = yes
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 6 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.160.a
	}
}

# 162 - John Glenn
country_event = { #Glenn Inauguration
	id = USA.162
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.162"}
	title = USA.162.t
	desc = USA.162.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_gln_inauguration

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
			promote_character = USA_John_Glenn
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.712
					days = 1
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter  min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD
			set_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD_Past
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = liberal_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Al_Gore_Sr_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Nelson_Rockefeller_pol
			add_ideas = USA_Jacob_Javits_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Cyrus_Vance_mil
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_68_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_GLN_68
			if = { #Check if the response mission should activate
				limit = { #Either Bennett or Wallace was elected
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP_Past
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			}
			else_if = { #RFK fucked up
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP_Past 
					has_idea = tno_minorities_segregation
				}
				country_event = { id = glenn.152 days = 30 }
			}
			country_event = { id = USA.neo_silver.1 days = 117 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nasa_funding_annual }
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.162.a
	}
}
# 163 - Michael Harrington
country_event = { #Harrington Inauguration
	id = USA.163
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.163"}
	title = USA.163.t
	desc = USA.163.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_people

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
			promote_character = USA_Michael_Harrington
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.713
					days = 1
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_crisis_counter = 1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_crisis_counter  min = 0 }
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP_Past
			373 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = social_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Irving_Howe_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Glen_H_Taylor_pol
			add_ideas = USA_Douglas_Fraser_eco
			add_ideas = USA_William_Winter_mil
			387 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			370 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			set_country_flag = USA_mil_68_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_HAR_68
			if = { #Check if the response mission should activate
				limit = { #Either Bennett or Wallace was elected
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past
						has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP_Past
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_begin_response
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD_Past }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_LBJ_great_society_modifier }
			}
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_fatigue = 0 }

			set_variable = { USA_HAR_enthusiasm = 0 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm = 45 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_middle_enthusiasm = 60 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_enthusiasm = 75 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poverty_enthusiasm = 90 }

			set_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_influence = 80 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_middle_influence = 60 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_influence = 35 }
			set_variable = { USA_HAR_poverty_influence = 1 }

			#Give an enthusiaism bonus based on Harringtons electoral win margin
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_middle_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_poor_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }
			multiply_variable = { USA_HAR_poverty_enthusiasm = USA_HAR_win_margin }

			#Put in place some reasonable limits on middle and upper classess so Harrington doesn't start with 100% approval
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_HAR_rich_enthusiasm max = 75 }
			clamp_variable = { var = USA_HAR_middle_enthusiasm max = 90 }

			clear_variable = USA_HAR_win_margin #No need for this anymore

			USA_HAR_calculate_enthusiasm = yes


			set_variable = { USA_HAR_fatigue_event_count = 0 }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = USA.neo_silver.1 days = 117 } }
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 4 }
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.163.a
	}
}

##1964 debate events
country_event = { #CR veto
	id = USA.164
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.164"}
	title = USA.164.t
	desc = USA.164.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress_2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #it was unconstitutional after all
		name = USA.164.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = -0.02}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.02}
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = -0.01}
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.01}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity}}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01}
				}
				else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01}}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #This was a dirty trick, we cannot have politicans like this
		name = USA.164.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.02}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = -0.02}
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.01}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity}}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01}
				}
				else = { add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.01}}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #CR neutral
	id = USA.165
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.165"}
	title = USA.165.t
	desc = USA.165.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_congress1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #RD - This is too contentious to deal with now
		name = USA.165.a
	}
	option = { #NPP - This is the most pressing issue of our day, you must deal with it
		name = USA.165.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { NPP_candidate_party = 4 } }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.01}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { NPP_candidate_party = 6 } }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.01}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.01}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = USA.167
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.167"}
	title = USA.167.t
	desc = USA.167.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_color

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #We must clean up at home first
		name = USA.167.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 83} #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 84} #African American
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity > RD_R_bonus_popularity }
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { nationality = 82 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_RD_popularity_low
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows_low
	}
	option = { #NPP answer
		name = USA.167.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows_low
	}
}

country_event = { #Bennett - RFK - Direction of USA
	id = USA.173
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.173"}
	title = USA.173.t
	desc = USA.173.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_supreme_court

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Bennett
		name = USA.173.a
		add_to_variable = { USA_RD_Unity = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.1}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
						check_variable = { nationality = 87 } #Rockies
						check_variable = { RD_popularity > NPP_popularity }
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.15 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.1 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #RFK
		name = USA.173.b
		add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_Unity = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { NPP_popularity > RD_popularity }
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 82 } #Yankee
						check_variable = { nationality = 85 } #Steel Belt
						check_variable = { nationality = 88 } #Pacific
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1 }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.1 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African American
						check_variable = { nationality = 86 } #Southwestern
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			}
		}
	}
}


country_event = { #Alcatraz escape
	id = USA.174
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.174"}
	title = USA.174.t
	desc = USA.174.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_navy_hawaii

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Crush the Bund
		name = USA.174.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_alcatraz_crush
			random_list = {
				30 = { country_event = { id = USA.175 days = 4}}
				70 = { country_event = { id = USA.176 days = 4}}
			}
			378 = { #California
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.1}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #The prisons are safe
		name = USA.174.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = USA_alcatraz_safe
			random_list = {
				25 = { country_event = { id = USA.175 days = 4}}
				75 = { country_event = { id = USA.176 days = 4}}
			}
			378 = { #California
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.15}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.177"}
	title = USA.177.t
	desc = USA.177.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_navy_hawaii

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.177.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				90 = { country_event = { id = USA.181 days = 7} }
			}
			358 = {
				add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.5}
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.3}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Observe and control the KKK more
	id = USA.181
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.181"}
	title = USA.181.t
	desc = USA.181.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #crack the klan
		name = USA.181.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					OR = {
						check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
						check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African-American
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
				multiply_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.8 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #nice-xon
		name = USA.181.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 3 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { nationality = 83 } #Dixie
							check_variable = { nationality = 84 } #African-American
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }

			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.200"}
	title = USA.200.t
	desc = USA.200.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_university

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #give them aid
		name = USA.200.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 9}
		set_global_flag = icw_aid_from_america
		add_manpower = -16000
		send_equipment = {
			equipment = infantry_equipment
			amount = 1000
			target = IND
		}
		IND = {
			army_experience = 10
			add_ideas = IND_american_military_advisors
			country_event = {
				id = indian_war.118
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #no
		name = USA.200.b
		IND = {
			country_event = {
				id = indian_war.119
			}
		}
	}
}

			ideology = social_democracy
			popularity = 0.01
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }

				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA.1102 days = 7 random = 100 }
			country_event = { id = USA.1106 days = 100 random = 720 }
		}
	}
}

		}

	fire_only_once = yes

		}

			ideology = conservative_democracy
			popularity = -0.005
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democracy
			popularity = 0.015
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democracy
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_NPP_popularity_grows

	desc = USA.2000.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.2000.a
		add_ideas = USA_arpa_low_funding
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_misc_costs_add_1_percent
			hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { gdp_temp = GDP }
			multiply_variable = { gdp_temp = 0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { gdp_temp = 0.15 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_2000_misc_costs days = 90 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.2000.b
		add_ideas = USA_arpa_med_funding
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_misc_costs_add_2_percent
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { gdp_temp = GDP }
			multiply_variable = { gdp_temp = 0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { gdp_temp = 0.3 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_2000_misc_costs days = 90 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = USA.2000.c
		add_ideas = USA_arpa_high_funding
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_misc_costs_add_4_percent
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { gdp_temp = GDP }
			multiply_variable = { gdp_temp = 0.04 }
			add_to_variable = { gdp_temp = 0.6 }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_2000_misc_costs days = 90 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #McNamara Inauguration
	id = USA.1701
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1701"}
	title = USA.1701.t
	desc = USA.1701.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_presidential_podium

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
			promote_character = USA_Robert_McNamara
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.721
					days = 1
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_72_D_RD
			set_country_flag = USA_72_D_RD_Past
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = conservative_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Birch_Bayh_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Donald_Rumsfeld_pol #commented out due to nonexistence, back in asshole

			396 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_RD_R_name = 1 } }
#			set_country_flag = USA_mil_72_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_BOB_72
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.1701.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Jackson Inauguration #EPIC EPIC EPIC
	id = USA.1703
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1703"}
	title = USA.1703.t
	desc = USA.1703.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_usa_treaty

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_new_president_election = yes
			retire_country_leader = yes
			promote_character = USA_Henry_M_Jackson
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.723
					days = 1
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_72_C_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_72_C_NPP_Past
			386 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
			set_politics = { 
				ruling_party = social_democracy 
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = USA_Sid_McMath_dep
			add_ideas = USA_Frank_Church_pol
			add_ideas = USA_Augustus_Hawkins_eco
			add_ideas = USA_Arleigh_Burke_mil
			386 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_C_name = 1 } }
#			set_country_flag = USA_mil_72_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_SCP_72
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD_Past }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nasa_funding_annual }
			}
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 4 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.1703.a
	}
}

			clr_country_flag = reload_tree_yes
			USA_clr_presidential_flags = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_72_R_NPP
			set_country_flag = USA_72_R_NPP_Past
			395 = { add_to_variable = { senator_2_NPP_R_name = 1 } }
			set_politics = { ruling_party = national_socialism }
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				USA_Louis_Byers_dep
				USA_Generic_Vacant_for
				USA_Generic_Vacant_eco
				USA_Generic_Vacant_sec
			}
#			set_country_flag = USA_mil_72_tree_available
			load_focus_tree = USA_YKY_72
			set_cosmetic_tag = USA_you_really_fucked_up
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD_Past }
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = USA_GLN_nasa_funding_annual }
			}
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 5 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.1705.a
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = 7 }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
		}
		remove_ideas = USA_last_bastion_of_liberty
		USA_increase_depression = yes
	}
}

#173x- '64 Second Inaug
country_event = { #Bennett Second Inauguration
	id = USA.1731
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1731"}
	title = USA.1731.t
	desc = USA.1731.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_meeting_table

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.1731.a
		add_political_power = 100
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_president_reelection = yes
			country_event = { id = RD.1 days = 120 }
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.751
					days = 1
				}
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 2 }
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1732"}
	title = USA.1732.t
	desc = USA.1732.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress3

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.1732.a
		add_political_power = 100
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_on_president_reelection = yes
			country_event = { id = RD.1 days = 120 }
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.752
					days = 1
				}
			}
			USA_get_total_congress_votes = yes
			country_event = { id = USA.neo_silver.1 days = 117 }
			set_variable = { presidents_party = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			target = GER

country_event = { #Drops southern discontent
	id = USA.1801
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1801"}
	title = USA.1801.t
	desc = USA.1801.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_whitehouse_bnw

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.1801.a
		USA_decrease_south_discontent = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Checks if Jim Crow is still around in the 70s
	id = USA.1803
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1803"}
	title = USA.1803.t
	desc = USA.1803.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_pentagon

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_idea = USA_jim_crow
	}

	option = {
		name = USA.1803.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP_Past }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_societal_unity_large
			add_to_variable = { USA_unity = -2 }
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = USA_subtract_societal_unity
			add_to_variable = { USA_unity = -1 }
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.1910"}
	title = USA.1910.t
	desc = USA.1910.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_presidential_podium

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = USA.1910.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = econ_decrease_money_reserves
		subtract_from_variable = { money_reserves = 0.100 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = USA.11000 #don't worry this is a debug event -uncountably
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.11000"}
	title = USA.11000.t
	desc = USA.11000.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "RD landslide"
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				can_have_elections_in_state = yes
			}
			multiply_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
		}
		set_popularities = {
			communist = 0
			socialist = 5
			social_democracy = 5
			liberal_democracy = 40

			conservative_democracy = 40
			authoritarian_democracy = 5
			despotism = 0
			fascism = 5
			ultranationalism = 0
			
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "NPP landslide"
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				can_have_elections_in_state = yes
			}
			multiply_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.1 }
		}
		set_popularities = {
			communist = 0
			socialist = 5
			social_democracy = 40
			liberal_democracy = 5

			conservative_democracy = 5
			authoritarian_democracy = 40
			despotism = 0
			fascism = 5
			ultranationalism = 0
			
		}
	}
}

#Ideas Tick Down Events

#Post-64 Elections and Primaries

country_event = {
	id = USA_elec_prim.1 #RD Primary 1968
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
		}
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_elec_prim.1"
	}
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			has_government = social_democracy
			has_government = authoritarian_democracy
		}
	}
	title = USA_elec_prim.1.t
	desc = {
		text = USA_elec_prim.1_RD_Incumb
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD
				has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = USA_elec_prim.1_NPP_Incumb
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_THURMOND_FR_NPP
				has_country_flag = USA_LEMAY
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_flag

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Barry Goldwater
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD
					has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD
				}
			}
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.1.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_LEADER_ROUTE_1968
					option = USA_LEADER_ROUTE_1968_GLENN
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { RD_candidate_party = 2 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 RD primaries: Goldwater"
		hidden_effect = {
			377 = { #AUH2O home state bonus for Arizona
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
				USA_debate_68_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #John Glenn
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD
					has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD
				}
			}
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.1.b
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1 
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = USA_LEADER_ROUTE_1968
					option = USA_LEADER_ROUTE_1968_GOLDWATER
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { RD_candidate_party = 1 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 RD primaries: Glenn"
		hidden_effect = {
			261 = { #Glenn home state bonus for Ohio
				set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.15 }
				add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = popularity_bonus }
				add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = popularity_bonus }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
				USA_debate_68_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #President Bennett
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.1.c
		set_variable = { RD_candidate_party = 2 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 RD primaries: Bennett"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
				USA_debate_68_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #President Johnson
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.1.d
		set_variable = { RD_candidate_party = 1 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 RD primaries: Johnson"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = USA_completed_first_primary
				USA_debate_68_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

	id = USA_elec_prim.5 #US Election 1968

	title = USA_elec_prim.5.t
	desc = USA_elec_prim.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_us_congress3
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = USA_debug_quadweekly_printing has_country_flag = USA_debug_printing_all } }
				USA_print_pop_to_log = yes
			}
			add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1}
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.12 days = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.161 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Goldwater"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.162 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Glenn"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.160 days = 75 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.17 days = 65 } #10 days before inauguration, MCS bennett meeting
				}
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Smith"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP }
				}

				set_variable = { USA_HAR_win_margin = NPP_electoral_votes }
				divide_variable = { USA_HAR_win_margin = 269 }
				country_event = { id = USA.163 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Harrington"
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD #LBJ 1 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.19 days = 35 } #LBJ Harry transition
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1731 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Bennett"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1732 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Johnson"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_FR_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1734 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Wallace"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					has_country_flag = USA_64_C_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1733 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1968 elections: Kennedy"
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { #Barry Goldwater
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.5.a
	}
	option = { #John Glenn

			}
			add_to_variable = { US_presidents = 1}
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.12 days = 30 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RD }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1701 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: McNamara"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1702 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: McGovern"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1704 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Kirkpatrick"
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD #Bennett 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.18 days = 15 } #Bennett-NPP transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD #LBJ 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.20 days = 30 } #LBJ-NPP transition
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP }
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1703 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Jackson"
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_D_RD #Bennett 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.18 days = 15 } #Bennett-NPP transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = USA_64_R_RD #LBJ 2 term
					}
					country_event = { id = USA.USA.flavor.20 days = 30 } #LBJ-NPP transition
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 5 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.1705 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Yockey"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 3 } }
				country_event = { id = USA.1706 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Hall"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RD
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1741 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Goldwater"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1742 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Glenn"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1744 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Smith"
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
					has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
				}
				country_event = { id = USA.1743 days = 75 }
				log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: 1972 elections: Harrington"
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { #Robert McNamara
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RD }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.a
	}
	option = { #George McGovern
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.b
	}
	option = { #Jeane Kirkpatrick
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.c
	}
	option = { #Henry M. "Scoop" Jackson
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP }
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.d
	}
	option = { #Francis Parker Yockey
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 5 } }
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.e
	}
	option = { #Gus Hall
		trigger = { check_variable = { US_election_winner = 3 } }
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.f
	}
	option = { #Barry Goldwater reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 2 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_D_RD
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.g
	}
	option = { #John Glenn reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 1 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_R_RD
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.h
	}
	option = { #Margaret Chase Smith reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 6 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_FR_NPP
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.i
	}
	option = { #Michael Harrington reelection
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { US_election_winner = 4 }
			has_country_flag = USA_68_C_NPP
		}
		name = USA_elec_prim.15.j
	}
}

#Class 1
country_event = { #Show preparation and mark states for election
	id = USA_election_helpers.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA_election_helpers.1"}
	title = USA_election_helpers.1.t
	desc = USA_election_helpers.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_big_meeting

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.2 days = 280 }
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.13 days = 100 } #Need to trigger way before the election, to show in the polls (societal unity)
			country_event = { id = USA_election_helpers.9 days = 60 }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #RDs
		name = USA_election_helpers.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_senate_elections_visible_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_can_campaign_for_RD_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_class_1_senate_prepare = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_campaigning_for_RD
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes

		}
	}
	option = { #NPP
		name = USA_election_helpers.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_senate_elections_visible_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_can_campaign_for_NPP_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			USA_class_1_senate_prepare = yes
			set_country_flag = USA_campaigning_for_NPP
			USA_recalculate_polls = yes
		}
	}
}

					set_temp_variable = { popularity_bonus = 0.05 }

country_event = { #The Insurgency is upon us
	id = USA.saf.effects.18
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event USA.saf.effects.18" }
	title = USA.saf.effects.18.t
	desc = USA.saf.effects.18.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_congress1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Fuck
		name = USA.saf.effects.18.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 150
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_OFN_unity
		add_to_variable = { OFN_Unity = 3 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Discontent_Fall_High
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_SAF_WAR_Discontent = 25 }
		clr_country_flag = USA_NPP_64_SAF_war
		USA_reload_presidential_tree = yes
		USA_increase_ruling_party_popularity_5 = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			if = { #NPP-C
				limit = { has_government = social_democracy }

				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.05 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.05 }
				}
			}

			else_if = { #NPP-FR
				limit = {  has_government = authoritarian_democracy }

				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1 }
					subtract_from_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.1 }
				}
			}

			else_if = { #RD-D
				limit = {  has_government = conservative_democracy }

				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_Y_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_D_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.1 }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1 }
				}
			}

			else = { #RD-R
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_L_bonus_popularity = 0.05 }
					add_to_variable = { RD_R_bonus_popularity = 0.05}
					add_to_variable = { RD_popularity = 0.1 }
					subtract_from_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.1 }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = USA_In_The_SAF_WAR
		TNO_fopo_remove_saw_tab = yes
		set_country_flag = USA_SAF_WAR_Insurgency_Activated
	}
}

					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 0.02 }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					can_have_elections_in_state = yes
					NOT = { check_variable = { NPP_popularity < RD_popularity } }
				}
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 0.02 }
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 00.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_C_bonus_popularity = 00.03 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = MADAGASKAR_OFN.5
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #
		name = USA.madagascar.7.d
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
			    factor = 0
			    has_game_rule = { rule = MAD_POST_WAR_PATH option =  MAD_POST_WAR_PATH_STOPH }
			}
            modifier = {
			    factor = 0
			    has_game_rule = { rule = MAD_POST_WAR_PATH option =  MAD_POST_WAR_PATH_SCHOEPS }
			}
			modifier = {
			    factor = 0
			    has_game_rule = { rule = MAD_POST_WAR_PATH option =  MAD_POST_WAR_PATH_RABEMANJARA }
			}
		}	
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { can_have_elections_in_state = yes }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_popularity = 00.02 }
				add_to_variable = { NPP_FR_bonus_popularity = 00.03 }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = MADAGASKAR_OFN.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = USA.senate.deaths.9.a
		if = {
			limit = { 951 = { check_variable = { senator_1_RD_D_name = 0 } } }
			951 = { add_to_variable = { senator_1_RD_D_name = 1 } }
		} else = {
			951 = { subtract_from_variable = { senator_1_FR_NPP_name = 1 } }
		}
	}
}
